======================================================================
EPISODE: S1E01
======================================================================

The episode begins with Elliot saying "Hello friend", to his imaginary friend, the audience. He tells them that what he is about to say is top secret, a conspiracy about the top 1%. He thinks that they are following him. He sees two men dressed in black talking and looking at him. He thinks that they are following him because of what he did the previous night. He thinks that he should have gone to Angela 's birthday party.
A flashback shows him at Ron's Coffee Shop . Elliot approaches the owner, Rohit "Ron" Mehta , who has just entered the shop. Elliot informs Ron that after observing the traffic on Ron's network, Elliot decided to hack him. Elliot discovered that Ron had been running a child pornography website, and had been using Tor to keep the servers anonymous. Ron seems shocked, and is noticeably shaken by the confrontation. Ron thinks that Elliot is trying to blackmail him and refuses to give any money, thinking that Elliot would keep asking for more and eventually tell the police anyway. After Elliot tells him that he has anonymously tipped off the police about Ron, Ron attempts to pay him off, but Elliot refuses by telling him that he doesn't care about money.
At the subway a man asks him what's happening, which Elliot ignores. The man then says "Exciting time in the world right now. Exciting time".
Elliot enters the Allsafe Cybersecurity offices, where he works as a cybersecurity engineer. Before he can reach his desk, Gideon Goddard calls him into his office, where Elliot meets with Angela. One of their clients, E-Corp , has been attacked again, and they are sending a group to hear exactly what happened during the attack.
After leaving the office, Angela confronts Elliot about him not going to her birthday party, saying that he promised he would try to. A flashback shows Elliot at the door of the location of her birthday party, but then Angela brings him back, saying "Stop thinking about something else when I'm talking to you". Eventually the conversation deescalates when Ollie appears, and Elliot leaves them.
At his therapist's office , Elliot tells his imaginary friend on how easy it is to hack Krista. He discovers that she is divorced, looking for a partner online, and is currently dating Michael Hensen , who Elliot finds little about. She asks him "What is it about society that disappoints you so much?" and Elliot explains, though only in his head, his anti-capitalism views and how he thinks that social media, celebrities and movies are mostly a method of sedation. After sitting quiet for a while, Elliot tells her not to be frustrated, because she at least understands what it's like to feel alone, that she wants to protect people from it and that's what he respects about her. When Krista asks him why he thinks she understands (since he discovered it by hacking her), he says that he doesn't know how.
Back at Allsafe, Ollie asks Elliot if he wants to have lunch with him. Elliot tells him that he already has plans. Ollie tries to tell Elliot that he feels things have been awkward between them, and that he wants them to get along. Elliot simultaneously tells his imaginary friend about Ollie: amongst his Facebook likes, Elliot finds George W Bush's Decision Points , Transformers 2: Revenge of the Fallen and the music of Josh Groban. Elliot thinks that that's enough not to like Ollie, but then adds that after hacking Ollie he found that Ollie had cheated on Angela multiple times with Stella B . Elliot says that he thought about telling Angela about this but he is not ready to see what "comes after". Back in their conversation, Ollie says that he likes Elliot and wants him to like him too. Elliot responds that he will try harder.
Elliot thinks that he shouldn't really hate Ollie, because he is not that bad, he is, rather, too dumb to be bad. Elliot says that when he thinks about the really bad people. That's when people from E-Corp arrive, he thinks about "Evil Corp". This is how Elliot has "reprogrammed" his mind to hear, see or read their name when they appear.
After E-Corp staff pass by him, Elliot thinks that Terry Colby , E-Corp's CTO (Chief Technology Officer) is a moron, an arrogant moron and unqualified for his job, using a Blackberry as his phone. Here Tyrell Wellick meets Elliot. He notices Elliot's use of Gnome , a desktop environment for Linux. Tyrell says that personally he uses another, KDE , what might seem unusual since he is an executive, but as he says "old habits, they die hard". He leaves Elliot after saying that "it's gonna be fun working with you".
After work, at Elliot's apartment, we learn that he's depressed and uses morphine to handle his life. He says that he keeps his usage lower than 30 mg (milligrams) per day while taking suboxone , a drug for patients on withdrawal or used for treating opiate addiction. He notices his stock of the latter has ended and calls his next-door neighbor Shayla for more. She offers it for free but he refuses. She asks if he wants to do molly (ecstasy) with him and the next scene shows them naked in bed, Shayla sleeping and he smoking. He gets an alert from Krista's Instagram that she is in Pierre Loti with Michael.
He finds Michael's address by using social engineering on the taxi company, saying that he forgot his keys in a car. While he watches Michael and Krista from afar, he sees the men in black watching him from a table across the street. When Michael leaves, the man from the subway comes to the table where the men in black are sitting and asks for any spare change. When Elliot eventually meets with Michael, he asks him for his phone to "call his mother ", when he actually calls himself to get Michael's number. Then, Elliot quickly deletes his number from Michael's call log.
He gets a call from Angela asking him to go to Allsafe because of what appeared to be just a DDoS (Distributed Denial of Service) attack against E-Corp. Elliot arrives there and finds out, that the servers are infected with a malicious software that can do practically anything on the servers by that point. Elliot says, that the only way to fix it would be to shut down the servers, clean the infection, and turn them back up.
Gideon and Elliot fly to the Dulles server farm to clean the infection. Elliot starts to examine the infected server and then identifies a file labeled fsociety00.dat, along with a text file (readme.txt) reading "LEAVE ME HERE" referring to the malware, the dat file, or both. Elliot says to himself that he's going to shut them down anyway, but then, he hesitates, he asks himself "What's wrong with me", and enters "N" to cancel the deletion. He stopped the hack by reconfiguring the access to the "root directory" (main, head folder), so only he can use it. Elliot is sure that "No one will know".
After leaving the server farm, at the plane, Gideon reveals to Elliot that he is gay, saying that even though he doesn't like to talk about his sex life, his partner wants him to be more open about it. Gideon seems stressed about the hacks so Elliot tells him not to worry, and explains, that hackers have short attention spans and will eventually harass someone else. Gideon feels that his company would have to go out of business if E-Corp left them. Elliot promises that he will find the hackers.
At the subway, the mysterious man from before sits in front of Elliot. His jacket has a marking with "Mr. Robot" written on it. He says that Elliot should come with him, but only if he didn't delete "it", referring to the hack. On the station, the man tells Elliot about his father who was a thief, got arrested, and died five years later. He thought that his father was free by stealing but actually he was in a "prison", just like Elliot is now, he says. The man is confident he will break Elliot out. They go to Coney Island where "Mr. Robot" shows him the other hackers on his team but does not disclose the plan.
Elliot goes home by himself and meets Angela at his door. She invites him to get high and watch Elliot's favorite movie Back to the Future II . When they went inside, they found Shayla still sleeping naked in his bed. Angela leaves irritated and Elliot tells Shayla to leave as well. Elliot tries to find information about fsociety and Mr. Robot but finds very little. He then puts all of the found data in a white envelope as evidence for Gideon and E-Corp. Elliot goes to Coney Island and talks with Mr. Robot again. He tells Elliot that their plan is to destroy E-Corp's databases so that they can erase most of the world's consumer debt. Mr. Robot tells him to put Terry Colby's IP address on the .dat file to make him appear responsible for the hacks. At home Elliot researches the effects of debts and decides to create another envelope, a blue one, which then he puts in a backpack with the white one.
At Allsafe, Elliot meets with Angela, Gideon, the executives from E-Corp and agents from the FBI . He places the white envelope at the table. After Colby treats Angela rudely, Elliot changes the white envelope for the blue one, in which Tyrell notices and gives it to the FBI, saying that with that they can find whomever is guilty of the hacks. 19 days pass and there is still no news from the FBI. The team from fsociety are not in the Coney arcade anymore. He decides to continue his attempt of hacking Michael Hansen but again it results in nothing. He realizes that this isn't his real name. In the next scene Elliot confronts Michael saying that he learned that he cheated on his wife with 7 different women and that he has proof of this. He demands that Michael breaks up with Krista and tell her the truth, otherwise he will tell everything his wife and the police, for one of the women was 15 (though Elliot explains to his "friend" that this last part was a lie). Michael agrees and Elliot asks also for his dog to help him with his loneliness.
In his next meeting with Krista he can see that she has been crying and that this must be because Michael told her the truth and broke up with her. Elliot meets with Angela and while they are talking, there is a newsbreak about Terry Colby's arrest for his supposed involvement with the hacks. While Elliot cheers outside, some men dressed in black tell him to get into their car and take him to a conference room. There he sees Tyrell Wellick, who is accompanied by other business man. They look like the one percent of the top one percent, what scares Elliot. Tyrell greets him with " Bonsoir, Elliot " (good evening, Elliot).
Elliot asks his imaginary friend "Please tell me you're seeing this too".

======================================================================
EPISODE: S1E02
======================================================================

Elliot watches as a group of men in suits sit at a round table with Tyrell Wellick at the head. "Give a man a gun and he can rob a bank. Give a man a bank and he can rob the world", Tyrell says. He explains that he likes this saying because it means that power resides with those who take it. He tells Elliot this meeting may be illegal, so he has gathered 11 lawyers, and offers Elliot to be the head of Cybersecurity for E-Corp . Elliot asks to think about it.
Tyrell dismisses the lawyers. Alone, he tells Elliot that he is on his way to becoming CTO and would like to thank the hackers who took down his predecessor, Terry Colby . He informs him that E-Corp will be internalizing their network by the end of quarter, so Allsafe will be cut loose and go out of business, thus Elliot should be with him. Elliot declines.
Elliot is driven home by Mr. Sutherland , who gives him a number to reach Tyrell. Walking to his apartment, Elliot comes across his neighbor/drug dealer Shayla bickering with Fernando Vera . As he drives away, Shayla tells Elliot that he was just an employer that can't take a hint. Elliot asks for a refill, but Shayla is hesitant because she doesn't have withdrawal meds to go with it. Elliot insists anyway.
At home, Elliot snorts some of his morphine, then goes to work hacking Tyrell. He finds that Tyrell's password to E-Corp's mail system is trivial, and starts to look through the mail and then comments to the viewer that this was too easy, its as if Tyrell expected Elliot to hack him. Panicked, Elliot pulls the memory chips, disk drives, and other components from his system and destroys them (microwaving chips, drilling holes in disk drives). He puts all of the ruined bits into a trash bag and goes out and tosses it into a subway station trash bin.
Elliot arrives at Allsafe, where he wonders if everyone is looking at him, but their attention is on the office TV which is showing news of the arrest of Terry Colby. Elliot wonders to the viewers whether he destroyed Colby's life just to advance Tyrell.
Gideon calls Elliot in and gives him a raise, a recognition for saving the company, but Gideon is curious about the dat file, and why Elliot didn't talk about it at the meeting. Elliot tells the viewer he's worried about how much Gideon is suspecting, but says that he wasn't yet really sure if the dat file was anything else, it could have been junk. Gideon however is satisfied, but wants Elliot to keep investigating, since the fsociety hackers could do anything. Elliot is alarmed: how does Gideon even know the name "F Society"? Gideon shows him a video that the group just released.
In the video, a figure in a mask and with a filter-distorted voice represents "F Society". It addresses "Evil Corporation", and says they "we" have been watching, "we" know how evil E-Corp is and all that it has done to oppress humanity, and "we" have collected tons of data stolen from E-Corp's systems, dirt that would bring down E-Corp if released. And they will release it, unless their demands are met: the release of their leader Terry Colby, the freeing of all of the debts of the world's debtors, and the dismantling of E-Corp. "The people of the world no longer accept your economic slavery".
Outside on a busy sidewalk, Angela and Ollie run into Elliot. (Nearby, there's a guy handing out his music CD's, free, he only wants people to like him on social media.) They congratulate Elliot on saving the company, and invite him to dinner. Elliot pauses, uncertain, and then notices in the crowd two men in black coats, looking like E-Corp security men, moving towards him. He quickly accepts their offer and hurries off home. (Angela and Ollie pass by the CD guy and Ollie accepts a CD from him.)
Elliot gets home, and he's telling the viewer that he's worried about the fsociety hackers and the data dumps they have from E-Corp, what they were talking about with freeing Colby, none of that was anything he had heard fsociety was doing. He needs to cut his ties with them. But in his apartment he discovers one of the fsociety hackers, Darlene , using his shower to take a bath, as if she had every right to be there. She borrows some of his clothes, saying hers are in a washer, and says Elliot had been expected to come last night, the others are expecting him later today. She seems strangely familiar with him, but he pretends that he doesn't know her at all.
Elliot and Darlene take the subway to Coney Island. He asks her how it is she knows him, but she assumes they know each other, it's only natural she knows where he lives and all that. Elliot remarks to the viewers that she's just weird, or crazy, if this is fsociety, maybe he should go to Gideon and tell him everything. She switches him to another train just ahead of the two E-Corp security men following them, he tells the viewers that it's as if she can see them too, they're not a hallucination.
They get to the fsociety hangout on Coney Island, and the other hackers, Mr. Robot , Leslie Romero , Mobley , and Trenton , applaud him, and say he did a good job. But Darlene asks Mr. Robot about the " Steel Mountain plan", and he says it's not ready. They all go do different things, and Mr. Robot and Elliot talk.
Mr. Robot says they have a plan: E-Corp, and many other evil corporations, maintain backups at Steel Mountain, that's a secure place, what we can do is, Elliot can use his Allsafe clearance to hack the Comet natural gas plant near Steel Mountain, we're working on what to do there to cause a natural gas explosion that will destroy the Steel Mountain facility. Elliot is aghast at this, and asks if the other hackers know this plan, and Mr. Robot says Elliot is the first.
This is way outside Elliot's comfort zone, he says he's not killing anyone. As Elliot goes to leave, Mr. Robot asks, "are you a one or a zero? Are you a yes or a no? Are you going to act or not?" Elliot refuses: "Life's not that binary." But Mr. Robot continues: "Beneath every choice, there's either a one or a zero." Elliot leaves, though Mr. Robot says, if he leaves, he's gone from the group, don't come back.
During a subway trip home, Elliot wonders to the viewers whether he should turn fsociety in.
He arrives home and checks in at Shayla's, and only discovers Fernando Vera there, dressed only in underwear, and he says Shayla is in the tub, and doesn't disturb her. They talk, Elliot uncomfortably, about Elliot's drug use, while Elliot explains to the viewer on what he's found about Vera: he's the "worst human being he's ever hacked", running drugs, porn, and guns, and his e-business is terribly unsecured, so the evidence of all that, including killing rivals, is all available. It would be easy to turn Vera in, but he's Shayla's only supplier, so Elliot needs him. Vera gets dressed and leaves, leaving behind the hint, backed up by his gun: Shayla is his.
Once Vera is gone, Elliot breaks into the bathroom, and finds Shayla bruised and drugged out in the tub. She says Vera came over, they smoked some, and that's all she remembers; it's clear she's been drugged and raped. But she doesn't want Elliot to do anything about Vera, she needs his money.
Elliot walks the streets, musing to the viewer on how Mr. Robot is right, we have to pick yes or no. He could do nothing, keep getting his drugs from Vera and Shayla; but Vera kills people, and has just raped Shayla, Elliot says he has no choice.
Elliot is at an appointment at Krista 's office, and he's complaining about "everything", about not being in control, not having choices worth making. (Throughout, this scene is interspersed with scenes of him doing web search into Vera's crimes with drugs and guns.) We think we can make choices, but they're trivial, like which of two drinks we want, but none of it really matters. (Elliot is shown uploading a file to an NYPD Anonymous Tip Line website.) It's as if the choices we make are predestined. (Now we see Elliot walking along a street, and there are Vera and several others, handcuffed and surrounded by police, as other police load evidence into a van.) Elliot tells Krista he had been in a "project", which he thought could have been special, but it turned out to be a mistake, might as well have done nothing. Krista says that Elliot had earlier talked about how his father had similarly chosen to do nothing about his cancer, or the company that gave it to him, and that he had no options, but Elliot now has options. Elliot gets upset and won't talk about his father, or anything else.
At home, Elliot is burning his Vera files onto a CD, and labeling it as music. His phone rings, it's Angela, he ignores it.
At home, Angela hangs up the phone, and tells Ollie she's worried about Elliot, he's been seeming out of sorts at work. Ollie is busy at his laptop, he's been trying to insert the CD he was given earlier, but he complains that it just freezes his computer. He checks his email, and there's mail from Stella B , with a picture and a message "come over tonight". Ollie takes care that Angela not see this, and tells her that he needs to go out and meet with a buddy who is unexpectedly in town. He leaves, but his laptop is still on, with its camera facing the bathroom where Angela is.
And now we see the CD guy, sitting in a library, looking at his laptop screen, which is showing what Ollie's laptop sees. Angela moves out of the camera view, so the guy closes the window. He opens another window that seems to be a chat in Chinese characters. He adds a line to the chat, in Chinese, but a subtitle translates it: "(Cisco) we're in".
The next day, Elliot is out walking on the boardwalk along the ocean, and finds Mr. Robot sitting on the railing. Elliot sits with him, looking over the rock-strewn beach. Elliot says he's come up with a plan to destroy the Steel Mountain backups without using an explosion. Mr. Robot doesn't want to hear about it until he gets past an issue. Elliot walked away, and now wants back in. He needs to hear from Elliot about his father. With some reluctance, Elliot explains that his father was his best friend, he worked at E-Corp all his life until they suddenly fired him, then he developed leukemia. He made Elliot swear not to tell anyone, not even Mom , even though he got sicker and sicker. Eventually he got so bad that Elliot told his Mom, and that got Dad so angry that he pushed Elliot out of the window, and Dad never spoke to Elliot after that, to the day he died.
Elliot asks Mr. Robot, so, are we good now? Mr. Robot nods and puts his hand on Elliot's shoulder. He says he knows what it's like to lose a parent, but did Elliot ever think he deserved what Dad did to him? Elliot says no, he didn't do anything, he was trying to help. Mr. Robot pushes Elliot off the railing, unto the rocks below. Mr. Robot comments to the air, "You didn't commit to the sacred pact you'd formed", and walks away.

======================================================================
EPISODE: S1E03
======================================================================

Tyrell Wellick is preparing a speech as he goes about starting his day, he is exercising, dressing, but throughout he is mentally rehearsing and refining a speech to give to the E-Corp CEO. The company is doing well, but there are challenges ahead, and we need a good CTO, and I should be that CTO. He practices in front of a mirror, over and over: "You will be the next CTO of this company".
Tyrell is sitting in the CEO's waiting room, mentally repeating over and over, "You will be the next CTO of this company". Finally, the CEO, Phillip Price , comes out of his room, but before Tyrell can start his speech, Price says effectively "you'll need to reschedule your appointment, there's a CTO candidate that the board is very excited about, we'll keep you informed, maybe I'll see you in a few weeks". Price hurries off, leaving Tyrell with his promotion speech unsaid.
Tyrell looks dejected as two E-Corp security men drive him through town. They stop at a street corner, where there's a homeless man waiting for them. Tyrell meets the man and pays him $300, takes off his coat and tie, puts on rubber gloves and proceeds to beat the man bloody, the man just taking the hits without any attempt to defend himself. Tyrell's guards just wait by the car until he is done. They drive him home, leaving the homeless man writhing on the ground.
Elliot wakes up in a hospital bed. He muses to the viewer on how debugging is not about fixing a mistake, it's about finding the bug and understanding why it was there to begin with, the bug exists to give the viewer a message. Elliot is bandaged and bruised, but wakes enough to recognize Shayla and Krista . He tells them that he was jumped by a bunch of kids. Krista wants to keep him in the hospital for a drug test, and suggests rehab, but Elliot says he's not an addict. Krista says she'll release him if he passes a drug test. Elliot remarks to the viewers that this is no problem, he uses this hospital because it has pitiful network security, he can easily change any of his medical records or test results.
Out of the hospital, Elliot and Shayla stop at a convenience store, where Elliot immediately snorts some morphine. They find that the credit card system at the store is down, due to the fsociety hack on E-Corp. Elliot remarks just to the viewer that he, Elliot, was the bug that fsociety found and is taking advantage of.
Shayla asks if Elliot had anything to do with Vera getting busted, Vera was Shayla's income, but Elliot denies any involvement. At home, he finds Darlene there, wanting to talk, but Elliot just tells her to get out. To Shayla's surprise, Elliot gets himself ready to go back to work that day, to the viewers he says, a bug is never just a mistake, it represents something bigger.
Out on the street, Angela is jogging, and a man runs past by her, dropping a wallet. She picks up the wallet and runs after him, shouting "Sir! Sir! You dropped your wallet!" He comes back and accepts the wallet from her, and runs off. Just as a young woman comes up saying he stole her purse, that was her wallet that Angela gave back to him.
Ollie is at home, looking at his laptop, and an email, "We own you and you will do what we want", the mail includes pictures of Stella B and an mail from her. Ollie is on the phone to Stella, saying "he wants me to put the CD on one of the computers at work". But Angela comes home, and Ollie hangs up the phone. Angela talks about running and the wallet, and Ollie smiles, this shows how good a person she is. She goes for a shower, and the phone rings for Ollie, a voice saying "You have one hundred hours, after that we'll release everything".
The scene switches to Cisco on the phone. After he hangs up, he goes to his laptop chat window, and adds another line in Chinese: "He'll break soon". Cisco continues to watch Ollie through the laptop camera, as Ollie paces around the apartment.
In Gideon 's office at Allsafe , he is giving directions to Elliot, Ollie, Angela, and Lloyd , on things to monitor to track down fsociety, in hope that fsociety makes a mistake. Elliot remarks to the viewer that the world we live in has us relying on other people's mistakes, to manipulate us. Gideon goes on to invite the team to his place for dinner tonight, and all accept except for Elliot. Gideon sends everyone else out and tries to talk with Elliot, his injured appearance and irregular attendance cause concern, but Elliot doesn't want to reveal any of his personal life.
Elliot tells the viewers that Mr. Robot may have found the bug at Evil Corp, but hasn't found Elliot's bug, it's the way he protects himself, closing himself off where nobody can find him. He gets to his desk, and there's Mr. Robot, waiting for him. Elliot doesn't want to talk to him, but Mr. Robot gives him the choice of having a scene here at the office, or having a drink at the bar next door.
Mr. Robot has a drink, but Elliot says he wants nothing to do with him. Mr. Robot says he's sorry for what he did to Elliot, and he never wanted to hurt him, he's sure Elliot's dad also wanted to apologize for what he did to Elliot, so Elliot shouldn't stay mad at him for too long. Mr. Robot gets up to leave, and Elliot is surprised on what about the plan? Mr. Robot explains, Elliot is the key, without him there is no plan, so it's over. He walks out.
Elliot is elated as he explains to the viewers that, with fsociety done away with, he's free from the "recent glitch in the otherwise neat reality" that he had created over the years. He'll strive to be more like a normal person, maybe have Shayla as a girlfriend, see Marvel movies with her, join the gym, like things on Instagram , drink coffee from Starbucks . "I'm gonna lead a bug-free life from now on, anything to protect my perfect maze."
Elliot returns to Gideon's office, carrying a Starbucks latte, and asks. Can I come to the dinner? And bring his girlfriend? Gideon says sure, but he's astonished, as if Elliot acting "normal" is unusual.
At Ollie's desk at Allsafe, he's almost ready to put the CD into his system, and sees Angela coming over. He pulls the disk out, they get their bags and leave.
Tyrell is at home, and is using his phone to investigate the Kiss and Fly Club, which looks like a gay hangout, and finds the club's page for Anwar Raziz , Philip Price's secretary. His wife Joanna , heavily pregnant, comes in. Tyrell says he's going out, to the Kiss and Fly Club. She's concerned, but he says it's for work, and necessary. She's still not sure, but he leaves anyway.
Elliot visits Shayla and invites her to the dinner party, and this actually gets her upset, first Vera used her and now Elliot is going to use her to look better in a social situation. She complains that he scarcely knows her (he remarks to the viewer that he knows her very well, he hacked her email long ago and knows all about her). Then she goes and starts showing her the artwork she's been working on, fabric and wall-art, all of it expressive in a way Elliot never knew. Elliot realizes he never actually knew her, she has her own maze, her own way of being at the fringe of society, like Elliot but in a different way. He explains to the viewer, that "when a bug finally makes itself known, it can be exhilarating, like you just unlocked something".
Outside the Kiss and Fly Club, Anwar and his friends exit, talking, when Anwar notices Tyrell waiting outside. Tyrell starts the conversation, as if he doesn't even know Anwar's name, but quickly gets to his being there, it's just to meet Anwar, because he's beautiful, and grabs him for a kiss. (Elliot tells the viewer. Because, after all, a bug's only purpose, its only reason for existence, is to be a mistake that needs fixing, to help you right a wrong, and what feels better than that?)
Elliot, Shayla, and the other workers arrive at Gideon's apartment, and stand around awkwardly until they are admitted. Gideon takes Elliot aside for a private chat, he says he had checked with Dulles again, and again there was nothing, he wants to make sure Elliot understands how valued he is. He even hugs Elliot (an awkward thing for Elliot), to reinforce in Elliot how he shouldn't doubt his skills and keep going, no matter the pressure Gideon puts on him.
After dinner, there is small talk going on around the living room. Angela and Elliot are sharing stories of their childhood together, with Angela, Elliot isn't awkward at all. But then the phone rings, and they turn on the TV to discover reporting of a new data dump of emails from inside E-Corp, revealing that the company knew everything about the 1993 toxic waste leak in Washington Township (that killed Elliot's father and Angela's mother ). The company, and Terry Colby in particular, were aware of the leaks, and decided not to spend money reducing them as it would not be cost-effective. Elliot tells the viewers: "My perfect maze crumbling before my eyes; there's nothing to hide behind". It's clear that fsociety orchestrated this leak to get Elliot back with them. "Mr. Robot finally found my bug". Elliot walks out of the apartment, quickly followed by a tearful Angela.
In a flashback, we see eight-year-old Elliot, and his mother Magda , both sitting at a bus stop. Elliot is sad about the death of his father, but his mother is nothing but dismissive of him, "he did this to himself, he gave in. He was a coward". When Elliot says he misses his father, his mother says there's no reason to, it just means Elliot is weak like his father. A bus comes by and stops. The voice of Elliot tells the viewer, "The bug forces the software to adapt, evolve into something new because of it. Work around it or work through it. No matter what, it changes. It becomes something new. The next version. The inevitable upgrade". The bus drives off, and now we see the same bus stop, but sitting there is only adult Elliot.
Tyrell and Anwar finish a violent session of anal sex together. Tyrell cleans Anwar some off and tells him to go take a shower. Once Anwar is in the shower, Tyrell goes and finds his pants, gets an SD card, and gets Anwar's phone. He boots the phone from the SD card and installs a superuser, connected to a web account. He puts the phone back into Anwar's pants, and goes to join him in the shower.
Ollie is pacing around his apartment, worried, when Angela arrives. Ollie is bothered that Angela will talk about things with Elliot but not with him. Angela says she will, but not right now. After some thought, Ollie says he has a problem, and shows her his laptop. She examines the blackmail message, and the pictures and screenshots attached to it, it details not only Ollie's relationship with Stella, but also information the hacker gleaned about Angela's bank accounts, and from that Angela's father 's bank accounts. For a while Angela says they need to break up, this threatens her father's finances, and she can't handle that. But she pulls back from that, and the figure they have to come up with something to do about this, but they don't know what.
Gideon is in his office, looking yet again at the report from the data center about the fsociety dat file, and the IP address highlighted on it, Terry Colby's IP address. He glances at a news report on his laptop, titled "Did Colby implicate himself?" It's 9:40 PM, it's late, but he picks up the phone and calls Dulles, and says he wants to talk to Sean Skyler about server CS30 again.
Tyrell gets home and finds Joanna in bed, with a mask over her eyes, they talk, and she's asking for some bondage sex tonight, even after Tyrell's night with Anwar. She is clearly in control of the situation, telling him what she wants tied up, and in what way. Elliot walks into the fsociety hideout. All of the other members are there, and silently watch to see what he does. He walks over to a table, gets out his laptop, and opens it up. Elliot is at home, musing on one last line of morphine in front of him. "The last line. The consequences of busting Vera and meeting Mr. Robot , creating you, everything till now, this moment. I chose this. I chose all this".

======================================================================

Elliot and Shayla are sitting at a table in a busy neighborhood restaurant. Fernando Vera 's brother, Isaac and Vera's homie D.J , watch from a nearby table. Elliot and Shayla aren't really eating, and not talking of anything important, just being together a little bit. They talk some about the first time they met, and Elliot wishes he could undo what's happened. He promises to get her out of this. Then Isaac announces that time's up. He then drags Shayla from the table and out of the restaurant (as the other diners take little notice). D.J stands over Elliot to keep him from objecting, and leads him to a back room.
In the back room, there's a telephone; Elliot picks it up, and it's Vera on the other end. Vera talks about some research he's done, research on his name and Elliot's: phrases like "brave traveler", "adventurer", "savage" come up. Elliot wants to know where Shayla is being taken, but Vera's mind is on other things: He's impressed with the power Elliot has, and he wants it, and by that he means he wants Elliot to hack him out of jail, today. Elliot says it takes weeks to find security holes, but Vera says it has to be tonight. And when they get back together out of jail, Shayla will be there too, Vera will give Elliot a big hug and they'll all be happy.
Elliot, Isaac, and D.J arrive at Elliot's apartment. Elliot is all worked up about Shayla, but Isaac wants him to concentrate on nothing but getting Vera out. As he looks at the documentation for the prison's control system, Elliot remarks to the viewers, that hacking a prison network isn't impossible, most are regular industrial control systems. Isaac and D.J are just hanging around, occasionally wondering what Elliot is good for, and whether he can do the job he's been ordered to do.
Elliot is curious about Isaac, something bugs him; he uses a wifi scanner tool, and finds a signal named "Isaac's S5 phone".
Angela is alone at Allsafe , it's before working time, nobody's there but her, and she's looking at the online article "Did Colby implicate himself?" She's also looking at the materials from the family's lawsuit from long ago, then she's printing out Terry Colby emails from the fsociety data dump, and going through and adding notes. That done, she gets a list of law firms, and starts calling them, asking each about the Washington Township scandal. She spends a while at this, getting nobody to talk to her, until she gets to attorney Antara Nayar . Now Allsafe employees are starting to arrive, but Angela sees that Antara Nayar has sent her a text; she gets her coat and leaves.
Outside the prison, Darlene is wandering around the parking lot, scattering flash drives on the ground.
Angela is meeting Antara Nayar in her office; Antara represented the 25 families of victims of the Washington Township case , one of which was Angela's mother. Antara says after the case was dismissed, she took eight years to rebuild her career. Angela wants her to reopen the case, with the new data that Angela has brought, but Antara dismisses the collection of "internet gossip" and amateur research. She turns Angela's attention to several clients in the waiting room, all serious criminals, but Antara will have an easier case defending them than if she again tried to attack E-Corp .
Outside the prison, an arriving officer notices the flash drives on the ground, and picks up one. We can see Darlene watching from a distance. Inside, the officer sticks the drive into a computer. It looks like he's in a security center, with many monitors on the walls. His computer shows him windows, offering him a free eTunes gift card, and he happily answers its innocuous questions ... until he gets a popup from the computer's malware detection system, it detected malware in the eTunes software. The officer is immediately anxious, first pulling out the flash drive, then pulling the power plug on the computer.
At Elliot's apartment, his desktop displays "Connection closed by remote host", he says he was in for a moment, but then the exploit stopped. Isaac slaps him and asks what's going on, but Elliot says he needs to take the dog for a walk. After Elliot leaves, D.J gets up and watches from the window as Elliot walks out of sight.
Elliot meets Darlene a block away, and complains that the exploit didn't work. She says, well, she only had an hour, it was all she could do, and he gave her no time to do it right. She's ready to walk away, but Elliot says Isaac and D.J are sitting on him, and he has to get this solved right away. Darlene is not impressed, but then D.J shows up. He shows them his gun, and waves them back to towards the apartment.
Antara Nayar still isn't willing to work further on the case, when Angela asks, "hypothetically", what it would take to make a case. Antara says it would take a reliable eye witness, an insider, who was there when the decisions were made. She doesn't think Angela knows anyone like that.
In an E-Corp meeting room, Scott Knowles is meeting senior employees, when Tyrell Wellick comes in. Tyrell says Scott should just skip the interviews and play golf with him, but Scott says he sees what's going on. Tyrell wanted to be CTO, he's not, and he's pissed. So Tyrell is trying to mess things up for Scott, but Scott says it won't work, he even knows the suggestions that went on between Tyrell and Scott's wife , she told him all about it. But Scott wants Tyrell to really get the idea. He's not going to be CTO, ever, so he doesn't need to play these "silly games".
Elliot is still researching, with Isaac and D.J watching over him and Darlene, when the doorbell rings, it's Angela. Though everyone ignores her, she keeps calling for Elliot to let her in, so Isaac lets Elliot go out and get rid of her.
Tyrell is at home with Joanna , he's furiously angry, while she is calm and confident. Joanna had told Tyrell that Scott was dangerous, and he is. Tyrell says he's at risk now, he has to pull back and remain patient. But Joanna reminds him that "patient" does not mean "cowardly". He has to take advantage of the opening that Sharon Knowles gave him. Sharon wants to be wanted.
Elliot meets Angela outside, and she says she's met with her lawyer, and has an idea on how to press the suit against E-Corp. She doesn't want to go into the details, which is fine with Elliot, he has urgent stuff to deal with that isn't her business, so he tells her to trust herself. She asks about Shayla, to which Elliot vaguely answers, and she leaves.
Elliot goes back up the stairs towards his apartment, and finds Mr. Robot waiting for him on the stairs. Mr. Robot warns Elliot that this thing he's doing for Vera, it can't work out well, it probably won't succeed, and whether it does or doesn't Vera's homies will probably kill both Elliot and Shayla anyway. Elliot says there's got to be a way, and he'll find it. Mr. Robot reminds him about fsociety, it's a success, and Elliot can do so much more with them, but this deal with Vera, it's failure.
Back at Elliot's apartment, he walks in full of purpose. He stuffs his laptop and other tools into his backpack, and says "I'm ready to bust Vera out". He needs to get to the jail, now, he wants Darlene to stay, but Isaac is having none of that, everyone is going.
On the way to the jail, Elliot thinks about how he misses his old life. "Remember when the panic would set in and we had a solution?" And now he has both Shayla and Darlene to rescue from Vera and his homies. Parked near the jail, Elliot gets out and marches in, quickly typing on his cellphone, thinking "My mind is frayed.... I can feel the static running through my brain".
Now Elliot is in the jail's busy visiting area, across the table from Vera. Elliot says he needs more time, but Vera says it has to be tonight. Elliot explains that, actually, he and Vera have to sit here and talk, because right now his cell phone is sniffing and detecting any sort of wireless network in sight, and then he'll own the network. Vera says, brave but stupid, when he springs Vera everyone will look to the security recording of this meeting and go after Elliot, but Elliot says he'll open all the cells at once, no problem. But, he knows, once Vera is free, he's going to need to run, and with his money too. Elliot has hacked Isaac's phone, and has hacked Vera's entire operation, crew, shipments, all of it, Elliot owns it. So he needs Vera's word: once this is done, Vera and his homies will leave both Elliot and Shayla alone, or else Elliot will leak his information. And in case Elliot just gets killed, he's arranged to leak it if he doesn't disable it every 24 hours. Vera doesn't look happy, but seems to accept it. He then tells him that he will hug him.
Angela tries to visit Terry Colby in his city townhouse. He doesn't want to be visited, nor dosen't want to talk to anyone.
Outside the prison, Elliot looks at his phone's snooping app, and it shows nothing but WPA2-protected networks. He thinks: "Borderline unhackable". But he stops and looks around at the parking lot, and runs another app, scanning for bluetooth transmitters, and finds one in a nearby police car. He realizes he doesn't need to hack WPA2, when there's a dedicated bluetooth network he can get into.
Elliot arrives at the car where the others are waiting: "We're good. I can pull this off". He's ready to get going, but Isaac pulls Elliot into the car, tells everyone else out, and drives off for a private talk.
Elliot and Isaac walk along the river, and Elliot is explaining, he's ready, he can free Vera, and if he doesn't he can kill Vera's operation. Isaac stops him and points his gun at him, Isaac is anxious, but Elliot is calm and understanding: Isaac doesn't want Vera free, he wants to have Vera dead, tonight, and the first thing Vera will do is to kill Isaac. Isaac is worried and puts down the gun. Elliot says Vera is all set either way, he's got protection inside, and if Isaac doesn't get him out, he'll have Isaac killed just for that. So Isaac's best choice is to let Elliot get Vera out, then Isaac can do whatever he wants. Isaac says, "What makes you think I still won't kill you afterwards?" Elliot replies, "I don't. I'm just playing my best move". Isaac puts the gun away, and they go back to the car.
Elliot explains to Isaac that he needs about a minute with the patrol car's bluetooth connection, and he'll have the exploit into the main prison control system, which will open all the cell doors at 9:49 PM. Darlene, dressed suggestively, approaches the officer in the car, and engages him in conversation. While she is keeping his attention on her, we can see windows pop up on the patrol car's laptop display, and we can see Elliot typing in commands. Elliot thinks, the exploit's in the laptop, now to get it into the jail. Elliot announces that he's paused the exploit, and they should drive away.
The police car gets a bulletin of an alarm going off, but Darlene keeps the officer distracted so he pays no attention.
In their car, Isaac points his gun at Elliot. Elliot says, "I only need to press one key to run the expliot. Or, I can press another and disable the entire plan. I made my move. You make yours".
The officer turns away from Darlene and notices the windows up on the laptop; he tries to type commands, but nothing works. The officer says he has to get back; Darlene walks away as the officer is calling in, "My computer's on the fritz".
Isaac lowers his gun and says they should go to the meet. They drive away. Elliot remarks to the viewer, if he made any mistake, the cell doors won't open, and he knows what that will mean. But doesn't make mistakes.
Night outside the prison, Isaac, D.J and Elliot are standing outside the fence. It's time. Isaac gets out his gun and tells D.J it's just in case some prisoner rushes them. There's noise, alarms, the screech of metal doors opening, and the campus lights go off. Elliot tells them it's from the power surge of opening all the doors at once, but the prison control system should still be saying all the cells are locked and closed, so the alarms will turn off. The lights come on again, and we can see prisoners boiling out from the buildings, headed towards the fence. They get through the fence door, and split in every direction, but it's Vera who walks to the three.
Vera tells them that this is just what he needs. Then he tells D.J to "shoot the cocksucker", and D.J shoots Isaac, who falls down dead. Vera says, that's right, he's his brother's keeper, and now "like Cain after Abel, I'll be a fugitive and wanderer on the earth". He thanks Elliot for his bravery, but tells him, his operation is over, Elliot can burn it to the ground, it doesn't matter he's gone.
A car drives up and stops next to them. As Vera and D.J move to get in, Elliot asks where Shayla is. Vera gets the keys to Isaac's car from D.J and tosses them to Elliot: "You just didn't realize she was with you the whole time". Vera and D.J drive off, leaving Elliot next to Isaac's car. He opens the trunk, and finds out that Shayla is dead, lying there. Elliot turns around, not quite crying, then definitely crying. We see the lights of police cars flashing around. He pulls up his hood and runs away.

======================================================================
EPISODE: S1E07
======================================================================

This was then, Elliot comes home and starts setting up a line of morphine, when he hears sounds from a new girl moving in next door, she calls herself Shayla , and dashes in for help. She needs a glass of water to save her black beta fish . She sits down on his couch, notices the line of morphine, and says to let her know if he wants a "top-shelf hookup". She asks his help in moving a dresser, and then they later go outside.
Elliot and Shayla make some awkward small talk. Elliot asks if Shayla can get Suboxone , her supplier doesn't have it, but she knows someone else who might. They take a few steps in getting to know each other, Shayla making the most effort. Oh, and Elliot can keep the fish.
That was then, and this is now. Elliot meets with Krista , thinking it's been a month since Shayla died, and he's annoyed that he's starting to get over her. Krista has some forms for him to sign, they say that he has completed the time with her that he needs. Elliot thinks she's trying to get rid of him. He wonders how much time he's spent with her and not listening to her. Krista says she does want him to keep coming, "We've got a lot more work to do", but Elliot gives her the signed papers and walks out.
Angela and Antara Nayar meet up with four lawyers working for Terry Colby . Angela wants a meeting with Colby, with no lawyers but Antara, to discuss information that Angela won't divulge but believes is beneficial to Colby. The lawyers are sceptical, but agree to pass the offer on to Colby.
Elliot is in Gideon 's office at Allsafe , and Gideon wants to offer Elliot some time off, to get over Shayla's death, Elliot feels that he doesn't need anything. Gideon advises him to find someone he can be his "honest self with". Elliot spends a while dreaming. In the old days of the web, kids like him could find someone else's website, view the source, and copy it into a new website, easy, so, what if you could "view source" on people? He imagines the other people in the office, with signs around their necks: "I got a nose job", "I pretend to love my husband", "I'm empty inside". Elliot finds the advice to find an "honest self" silly, but he thanks Gideon and leaves.
Darlene and Mr. Robot are in a bar, she is drinking and he is reading a paper. He's impressed by a story about "the hacker group fsociety ", it's like they made an impact, and he thinks they should get the Dark Army working. Darlene says she's tried, no go, they are experts and can't be hacked. Anyway, the tape backups are now in place, they have no way to get around that. Mr. Robot says that he's got a plan in motion.
Elliot is in his apartment, burning a CD with all of his Shayla files. "This is all I have left of her. I will miss her. I need to wipe again". He unplugs the computer's components, pulls the memory sticks, the hard drive, and carries the memory sticks to the kitchen to microwave. Unnoticed, a microSD card falls from the pile in his hands, and his dog snaps it back up.
Tyrell Wellick is meeting in his office with three of his executives, he's not paying much attention as they talk casually about budgets and earnings, and then gossip about lower-level executives who "go gay to move up the ladder", and others who "go cock jockey" for promotion. Tyrell looks like he heard that, and asks one of the executives about his children. After getting a response. Tyrell yells "You're fired!" Everyone is stunned, silent, then they smile, it must have been a joke. Tyrell says, "You two as well. I'm making sure you all receive the minimum severance packages". When the executives ask what they did, Tyrell shrugs: "Nothing".
Angela walks into Antara's office, and learns that Colby's lawyers wanted a promise of "total immunity" before the meeting, and Antara has just arranged that. So that Colby has agreed to meet privately with Angela. But Antara warns Angela, this may not be a good idea, she'll be in the home of a very powerful man, with a lot at stake.
Mr. Robot visits Leslie Romero at his home, he's been busy making up THC-based skin cream, he's got lots of clients. Mr. Robot wants Romero back into the fsociety project, but Romero considers it as a wasted effort. Mr. Robot alternates between threatening and cajoling Romero, and eventually Romero seems to accept that he has to get back with the group.
Angela meets with Terry Colby at his house, and he is initially dismissive of her, just asking how much money she wants. She says she has information than can help him, if he can testify about the E-Corp executive meetings that dealt with the hazardous waste issue. He is mostly obscene in his responses. He gets up to leave, but Angela stops him with the idea that, if he leaves, people will be left with the idea that he's guilty, and he'll lose their respect, and she is a way for him to get out of that.
Elliot has taken the dog, named Flipper, to the veterinarian. She scans the microchip on Flipper's back, to satisfy her housekeeping, and then she looks at the xrays. Flipper seems to have eaten something, perhaps trash, that is big enough to upset her insides. She will keep Flipper for a few days until it passes normally.
Angela is walking along the sidewalk, when her phone rings, it's Antara, Colby's lawyers called and said that Colby had agree to talk, right now.
Darlene meets Cisco at the library, and Cisco is still pissed, Darlene's attempts to lean on the Whiterose left Cisco looking like an expendable foot soldier. She hacked into Cisco's system and used Cisco's credentials on chat to talk to the Dark Army. So he doesn't want to see her again, but the Dark Army says the meeting's on.
Angela meets Colby at his house again, and he's going to provide the testimony, but he wonders what's in it for her? She doesn't actually answer, but asks again the question she asked before: was Colby at meetings where the hazardous waste issue was discussed? He says, yes, many of them. The issue wasn't a big deal for them, it wasn't a vile assemblage of gloating evil conspirators, it was just board meetings, people running a business. Sure, there was some realization that this wasn't the "right" thing, but then they moved on down the agenda.
The executives of E-Corp, and families, are meeting at night in a festive room, as Phillip Price toasts Scott Knowles as the new Chief Technology Officer. People mingle, many getting in line to congratulate Scott. In the background are Tyrell and Joanna Wellick . He is stealing himself for something, and she encourages him as she sends him off. Tyrell meets up with Sharon Knowles at the bar, and she expresses disappointment at how he still seems sore about what happened a month ago. Tyrell makes a bold suggestion, meet him, tonight, in his office, or better, the roof, the back stairwell cameras are out. She doesn't reply, but walks away.
Angela is in Gideon's office at Allsafe, and she recognizes that she needs to be fired, but his concern is that her revelations will ruin Allsafe, nobody will want to do business with them. And Angela needs to feel for the fates of all the Allsafe employees that will go down with it.
Sharon Knowles meets Tyrell on the roof, and they banter a bit. She says she came to see if Tyrell was really as gullible as he seems, with her husband downstairs getting the job that Tyrell wants. Anyway, she feels he's playing the game poorly. He says Sharon really needs Tyrell because she's dissatisfied with Scott, but she feels Tyrell is just desperate to cling to any chance to stay at E-Corp once Scott takes over. Tyrell grabs her and kisses her, and she kisses back. They go to the ground, kissing and groping, and he wraps his hands around her neck and starts to strangle her. She tries to yell, tries to struggle, but eventually she chokes and is later unconscious. Tyrell gets up, panting and sobbing. He stumbles away a few feet, then comes back to wipe her neck with a cloth. Then he runs away.
It's day, and Darlene meets Trenton outside. The plan with the Dark Army is back on, and Darlene needs Trenton to be back with the group. Trenton wonders what it is that motivates Darlene, and Darlene has no real answer, she just knows that somehow they've gotten together with the tools and the people to do the right thing, right now.
Cisco waits by a storefront until Ollie walks by, and Cisco follows. Ollie is put out of shape by this, and wants Cisco gone, but Cisco says Ollie is in no condition to complain. Ollie put a malicious CD into his work system, and Cisco and his fellas know it. Ollie just wants out of whatever this is, but Cisco says Ollie has to do what he's told, or "the giant shit storm that rains turds will leave a trail of clouds in the sky spelling out your name". Ollie nods.
Elliot goes and meets Krista at her office, it's before office hours but she lets him in. After she confirms that what he says will be kept confidential, he admits some things: He's been lying to her all along. He doesn't actually take his pills, but Krista doesn't either. He's been keeping track of her online presence, she bought a hazelnut latte this morning, she texted her sister about it, she's not good with money, she seems to be encouraging her Thursday 2:00 to leave her husband, she's tired of being dumped. She cries sometimes, just like Elliot. He says he doesn't just hack her, he hacks everyone, his friends and coworkers. But he wants a way out of loneliness, just as Krista does. "Is that what you wanted to hear?"

======================================================================
EPISODE: S1E08
======================================================================

It's morning in a nice apartment, and on the balcony is Darlene , with little in the way of clothing, looking out on the city. Her hookup, Xander Jones , already well dressed, comes out and holds her a bit. She talks a little about, "what if a revolution happened?" He's not into that sort of thing, he gets paid a lot to deal with problems. It's time for him to go off to work, he kisses her and leaves.
Once he's out of the door, Darlene comes back inside and searches the apartment for any hidden cabinets. She finds a safe hidden under the bar. Xander's MBA diploma is nearby on a wall, she puts in the graduation date as a combination... and the safe opens. Inside, she pays no attention to anything but a handgun, which she takes and puts it into her purse.
Darlene walks into a ballet studio, with lots of women stretching and practicing, and one of them is Angela . She's on the phone (" Ollie ... I don't care who you ran into or what he said,"), but hangs up as Darlene joins her, they are clearly old childhood friends. Angela assures Darlene that she's not getting back together with Ollie, he just has some work stuff to deal with. They discuss how Elliot's getting along. "He's had a shitty month". "Or twenty years". The ballet teacher arrives, and Angela and Darlene take their places in the class.
Elliot is thinking about Krista , and how he hurt her. "I don't feel good about that. I hope you're not mad at me". Elliot is burning a CD with his desktop's "Krista Gordon" folder, which he then deletes. He labels all of his hacked-person data CD's with the name of an album. Krista's gets labeled "Talking Heads Speaking in Tongues", and he adds it to his collection of CD's. He spends a while looking through the web page for AirDream Advanced Metering, they provide modern building automation services.
Elliot goes out onto the street and meets Mr. Robot . Elliot asks if Mr. Robot got everybody back, and Mr. Robot nods.
Darlene is on the subway, it's rather crowded, but she notices two asian men a little way down the car, looking directly at her. One nods to the other, and they get up and walk over to stand right in front of her, she puts her hand in her purse. One says, as if to his partner, "Tell him to follow the proper commands, or the sequence won't initiate". They both walk away down the car, and Darlene looks after them.
At the fsociety hideout, Elliot is telling everyone his plans. He remotely patched the software in the Raspberry Pi that he had planted in Steel Mountain , he's been monitoring it daily, it's all ready. His malware has been planted at all five of the Steel Mountain locations. They all use AirDream control systems for HVAC, and they are all networked together, so fsociety will arrange to heat all of the locations at the same time, while making sure no alarms go off from the temperature rise. Elliot gets a text from Lloyd Chong : " Allsafe 's been hacked".
Elliot needs to get to Allsafe, but then Darlene arrives to say that the Dark Army are following her, and probably will follow him as well. She hands him her gun, saying those guys are dangerous, and the meet with the Whiterose might not go as he wants. Elliot gives back the gun, he doesn't know how to use them. Darlene grabs his phone and dials herself from it, so they both have each others' number, that's not fsociety protocol, but she says he needs this now. Elliot leaves, and Darlene hides the gun in a popcorn machine in the hideout.
As Elliot leaves fsociety, Mr. Robot catches up with him, to say he should forget Darlene's number. But he's sure that the Whiterose wants to talk to Elliot, and he can't afford any distractions.
Tyrell Wellick is walking rather in a haze through the E-Corp executive hallways, he gets easily distracted by conversations, and walks into a fellow exec and spills his coffee. His assistant, Elizabeth , catches up with him. He tells her he's busy, cancel all meetings and hold all calls, but she says that Gideon Goddard is already in the office waiting to see Tyrell.
Gideon tells Tyrell that an employee broke the chain of custody with the Colby data file, so it can't be used as evidence against Colby. But Allsafe is putting in place many measures to find the hackers, such as setting up a honeypot for server CS30, the one that fsociety used for its last attack. At the mention of CS30, Tyrell is sweating, but Gideon goes on, Allsafe will ensure that fsociety can't cause any more damage. Just at that moment, Gideon gets a text from Lloyd Chong: "Call the office! 911! Entire network down". Tyrell makes noises of understanding Gideon's concerns, and thanks him for giving the problem his entire attention. They shake hands, and Gideon leaves.
As soon as Gideon is gone, Tyrell turns to his keyboard, and makes an ssh connection to server CS30, or presumably its honeypot. He searches for directories for which he has no access, and looks over the list, staring at one called "fd1info". He looks into that directory, and stares for a while at one file on the list, "fsociety". But then he is interrupted by his assistant. The police are here, there was a body found on the roof last night, and detectives want to speak with Tyrell. Tyrell gets up and says work has to go on, the detectives can make an appointment to talk with him, but for now he needs to talk with the Dulles server farm. He walks out of his office.
At the Allsafe offices, Gideon has gotten back, and is assigning tasks to various employees to get things running again. He tells Ollie to cancel all appointments, no customers can hear about this. He goes into the server room, just as Elliot shows up for work. Gideon and Elliot look at each other for a moment, then Elliot gets to work.
Elliot is looking at logs on his system, and commenting to the viewer. This hack is no big deal, the hackers already have a lot of control of the company systems but aren't doing anything actually valuable, it's like they are making a distraction, something that will keep Allsafe engineers busy while something else goes on.
Then Ollie comes by, and he seems nervous as he gives Elliot an assignment. Take these two disk drives to Blank's Disk Recovery to be destroyed, and right now. Elliot objects, he's working on the malware now, but Ollie pulls rank, Elliot has to do this right now, it's noon and the appointment at Blank's is at 2 PM, go get this done.
Elliot is curious about Ollie's nervousness, and hacks into the Allsafe mail system to look at Ollie's mail. His most recent Sent Mail has lots of messages to Angela, with subjects like "I'm on the verge of tears", and "This hack is your fault!" Elliot wonders what Angela has to do with this.
Tyrell is back at home with Joanna , and she's surprised, there's a gala tonight. She's sure that, last night, he slept with Sharon Knowles , and took pictures that they can use for blackmail against Scott Knowles . Tyrell says blackmail is too unpredictable, they have to find another way. She says blackmail is perfect, it would raise a scandal, and the company wouldn't allow a scandal during the earnings report, so Scott will resign and Phillip will name Tyrell as CTO. Tyrell has no answers for her and says nothing. She says, "Don't unravel now".
On the street, Elliot runs into Angela, and complains that she didn't tell him about what was going on with Ollie, Elliot could have helped. Angela says Elliot's not been around to help anyone for a month. Anyway, she says "some guy" gave Ollie a CD that infected his laptop, and the guy forced Ollie to run a disk at Allsafe, so that got done, a while ago. Elliot remarks to the viewers. I was right, the hack was a distraction, this is something set up by the Dark Army and something to do with me and this meeting. Angela is still bothered, Elliot hasn't been himself for several months, even before Shayla .
Elliot gets to the storefront of Blank's Disk Recovery. He thinks that the Dark Army has taken extraordinary steps to make sure this meeting's exactly how they want it. He goes in and gives his name.
Someone leads Elliot to a glass-walled room, and Elliot remarks to the viewer on how it is a Faraday cage, a room where no radio signals go in or out. Inside the room, there is a guy in a hazmat suit, eating a sandwich. The door is open, and Elliot walks in. As he does so, the guy walks out and closes the door behind him. Another door opens, and walks in is the Whiterose, an asian trans woman. She demands the disk drives that Elliot has, and starts to disassemble them. She looks at her watch, and says that she manages her time very carefully, she has allotted Elliot three minutes.
He starts to talk about the drives, then about the E-Corp hack that fsociety has ready to run, but the Whiterose dismisses such topics, they waste precious time telling her things she already knows. He asks if the Dark Army is ready to do their part, and the Whiterose says it's fsociety that is not ready. If they failed to have a worthwhile focus, first the hack to target Terry Colby, then the vulnerability that raised the suspicion of Gideon Goddard. So Gideon has made a honeypot of the hacked server. Elliot says he'll get rid of the honeypot, but the Whiterose says she's not inspired with confidence, until a few seconds ago Elliot didn't even know there was a honeypot. Now the Whiterose sets a deadline. Elliot has 50 hours and 23 minutes to disable the honeypot, and then the Dark Army will initiate the hack. She says Elliot will never see her again, and she walks out.
Elliot hurries along the sidewalk back to Allsafe, thinking on what he has to accomplish. He has to get the honeypot down, Gideon has been spying on Elliot, and it's Gideon who has the credentials to get the honeypot turned off. He realizes that he needs a distraction so he can get to Gideon's phone, he calls Darlene and records a message for her.
Back at his office desk, Elliot looks across the room to where Gideon is doing something on his phone. Elliot goes to the coffee pot, just as Gideon looks at the phone, plugs it into its charger, and leaves it on his desk. Elliot remarks to us about how he got a hundred large files transmitted to Gideon's phone, draining the battery. Elliot gets out his own phone, and texts someone a message: "Go".
In the conference room off of the desk area, there is a large TV set, and it starts displaying another of those fsociety videos, with a masked figure making pronouncements: "Corporate greed is a trickle down desire that reaches even the bottom of the food chain. And for what?" It's loud enough that all of the employees can hear it, and all of them rush to the conference to see what's going on. Except for Elliot. The video is specifically against Allsafe, and Gideon Goddard, and says that Allsafe's nightmare is about to begin, the sweet dreams are over, et cetera, et cetera, you will soon be finished. Some in the room are checking their phones. The video is also on YouTube, and on the Allsafe website.
But while everyone's attention is on the video, Elliot slips unseen into Gideon's office; he taps on it, ending with a display showing a code number. Elliot thinks that the passcode is only good for 90 seconds, he has to log in with it on his computer in that time. Elliot quickly walks to his desk. Just as Gideon, with the others in the conference room, looks around and says, "Where's Elliot?"
Gideon hurries across the room to where Elliot is sitting at his desk. Elliot types the passcode into the login screen for the IT Admin ticket system, logging in as Gideon, and he iconifies the window just in time for Gideon to not see it as he arrives at Elliot's desk. Gideon says he's quite suspicious of Elliot. All these events have been happening around Elliot's appearances and disappearances, and now, there's a disaster going on, every employee was in that room seeing it, and Elliot was off doing something else? Elliot has nothing to say. Gideon wants answers, but gets pulled away. E-Corp is on the phone, right now. Gideon goes, but says he's "not finished" with Elliot.
Elliot had indeed gotten logged in to the ticket system in time, and he finds the tickets Gideon used to establish the honeypot. He types in a new ticket: "Please remove honeypot and restore normal connectivity on server CS30". He remarks to viewer: When he hacked Gideon, and his secrets, he saw a good, honest man, Gideon is wrong, because Elliot really is "finished" here, he's not good for Allsafe or its people. He knows Gideon is protecting his people, but Elliot is doing this "to protect everyone".
Tyrell is in his limo, parked outside the fsociety hideout, talking with Mr. Robot. Tyrell knows fsociety has been busy, and wants to know what's planned, they and he are supposed to be allies. Mr. Robot disagrees, there's nothing they could agree on. Tyrell says he has a hold over Mr. Robot, Tyrell knows "your dirty little secret". Mr. Robot says they shouldn't be petty, and once Tyrell thinks about it, he'll realize that telling anyone about "that" does neither of us any good, and the only thing for Tyrell to do in his position is nothing.
Tyrell gets home, and immediately picks up a bottle and drinks deeply. Joanna notices, and says it doesn't inspire her confidence. She had heard that the gala was cancelled, and that maybe Tyrell had accomplished something last night, though he won't tell her what. Tyrell says it doesn't matter anymore, he and she have been blinded by focusing on the "wrong players". He says some months ago he met a tech guy, Tyrell thought he could use him to get something, but now he realizes that the tech could be the step to something grander and more beautiful: God. Joanna is dumbfounded.
At that point, the doorbell rings, and it's two detectives, Quattlander and Jones . They are investigating the murder at E-Corp, and want to talk to both of them. Tyrell tries to derail this, saying they should make an appointment at the office, but the detectives say this is a time sensitive matter, and they have questions that need answers. First, they ask, did the Wellick's know the deceased, Sharon Knowles? This floors Joanna: "Sharon Knowles? That's terrible. Yes, yes, we did know her". She invites the detectives in.
Inside, she offers the detectives coffee, they accept, and she goes to the kitchen. The detectives sit down with Tyrell, and ask him when did he last saw Sharon Knowles. Tyrell just sits and stares, long enough that the detectives ask whether he's all right. Then they all hear a groan from the kitchen. They rush in, and Joanna is leaning against a counter, there's a pool of blood on the floor between her legs. Tyrell says he thinks the baby is coming, they need to go the hospital. Jones starts calling on his phone. Tyrell notices, sitting on the kitchen counter, a 2-tined fork with blood on the end. He looks at her, wordlessly, and she says (in Swedish): "I will not let them take you. You will not leave us".
Night at Coney Island, and Elliot is sitting with Darlene. Darlene says the hack of the climate control system is all set up. They agree, they've done it, in 43 hours, exactly, the honeypot will go away, and her rootkit will take down Evil Corp. Darlene is ecstatic, Elliot really got them to do something worthwhile, and she says "I love you so much". At that, he leans forward and kisses her.
Darlene immediately pulls back in disgust: "what the hell is wrong with you?" Elliot sputters and apologizes, he's confused. "Oh my god, Elliot. Did you forget again? Did you forget who I am? Tell me who you think I am". Elliot is surprised: "You're Darlene. You're Darlene!" But Elliot thinks to the viewers: "I know. I know what she's going to say". She starts to say it: "I'm your..." and he finishes it: "Sister. You're my sister". He steps back, puts up his hood, and walks away.
Elliot makes his way home via subway, in a haze of "I remember Darlene", and "I'm crazy", and "Why did I forget?", and "I'm crazy". "Were you in on this the whole time?"
He gets to his apartment, still terribly confused. "Is this amnesia? What else am I not remembering? I should have stayed on the meds. I'm crazy. I should never have created you. Do I even exist?" The phone rings, he glances at it, then throws it across the room. He sits at the computer, uses a search website to find himself, nothing comes up. He tries the other search engines and people finders, no sign of the "Elliot Alderson" of New York who works with computers. "Nothing. No identity. I'm a ghost. Did I erase myself?" He goes to his CD folder and pages through them, reading some of the labels, glancing at a few and tossing them aside. He finds the first CD on the case, it has no label or name written on it, it's blank.
He puts the CD in his machine, and the folders appear. He pages through a directory of pictures, lots of pictures of a man who looks exactly like Mr. Robot, dressed differently, who seems to be an ordinary, smiling, relaxed man. Then there are pictures of this man, and the boy that Elliot remembers as him when he was young, this could be that they had father-and-son pictures? Lots of happy pictures of them doing things together. He remembers something, he gets up and finds on one of his shelves a picture, it's a family foursome picture, Dad (?), the woman Elliot remembers as his mother , his young self, and a young girl. Is it his family? There's a pounding on the door. It's Mr. Robot: "I think we should talk".

She's wanted justice, but they are an untouchable conglomerate. Even Mr. Robot's plan wouldn't win. Not until she meets the Whiterose, who opened her eyes. All the damage could finally be undone. A new world will be reborn. The streetlights turn on outside as the city regains power.

Over a period of 5 weeks, Elliot gets a job as a security analyst at E-Corp and works to undo Stage 2 and the fallen state of the world. He feels great creating a better E-Corp once it gets back on his feet.
One day, Elliot looks around the office and admits to the audience that he hasn't fixed everything. The loneliness came back. On Let's be Frank with Frank Cody at 8 PM, the host Frank Cody interviews Joanna Wellick . He also asks Irving to check on his wife and inform her of the plan, as online gossip about her has died down. Irving agrees to see to it. Finally, Tyrell says if Stage 2 is to proceed, he needs the full force of the Dark Army.
It's daytime, and Phillip Price is in a limo on the phone with Angela, who is in her apartment. She asks him to fire Elliot and ban him from all locations of the company. When he asks why, she says her reasons are her own and that she's good to return the favor. He says it will be done. In Angela's living room, Mr. Robot is at the table, confirming who he is and asking what happened. She recounts when Elliot saw her and Tyrell, but he's asking about the call she just made. Angela insists he stay for the weekend. She can handle Elliot when he wakes up while Mr. Robot fights him off. As he voices his concerns about Stage 2 derailing, she receives a text from Irving that it's on Monday.
Darlene packs her backpack in the empty apartment. She looks at the Polaroid and finds that Elliot isn't home, just Flipper. She puts the photo back on the shelf and leaves.

On 9/29, Elliot is riding the elevator up in the E-Corp building when a man staring at him says something in German. She invites him to lunch later.

At his computer, his coworker Samar Swailem remarks on the gathering of protestors outside before recounting another sex story. Elliot demeans him out loud; he meant it for his inner monologue. Samar's confusion and promise of silence turns into anger and then contrition for his behavior. Elliot ignores him. The VP of technology passes by, and Elliot at first thinks he had been rehearsing his proposal all weekend until he remembers that the meeting was last week.

Elliot determines that he should sneak back in the building and secure the HSMs. First he needs to evacuate the recovery building. In the lobby, security escorts him out.
Outside, the protesters chant that they are what democracy looks like. Elliot calls in a bomb threat to the building. Darlene meets him and as he begins to tell her his plan, she reveals that she has been working with the FBI . The guard becomes suspicious and insists she comes with him.

They talk a little bit and notice each other's IDs. The woman notices Angela is wearing gloves and gets suspicious. A rioter breaks into the room but is maced by the woman, who runs away. Angela completes the job and finds the rioter gone. She puts on a hoodie she finds hanging and a discarded and bloodied mask to traverse the hallways. Rioters loot the unconscious security guard and pay her no mind. On the elevator, she takes off the mask and sees Frank Cody on TV reacting to the news of China's success, supporting Donald Trump in the arms race of global superpowers. She calls Irving and tells him about the woman who saw her doing the job, explaining that she couldn't find Elliot in the riot as she was almost attacked. He assures her that they took care of it, that the Whiterose can make it all better, and to remember the cause. Back on floor 41, she meets the Hamburger Man and they exchange packages.
