Andy wonders if Elliot is with the police, looking to resell in the neighborhood, or finds his life unbearable. He comes on to Elliot a bit and surmises that Elliot has a death wish as well as calling him a cute boy.
Elliot knocks on the door of Sunil's brother Sandesh's house. Sandesh tells him to get lost, but Elliot insists on paying respects some place. Sandesh then starts grousing that Sunil has endangered Sandesh's job. Elliot tells him not to believe what's being said o the news. But Sandesh believes the news and refuses to pay for a "terrorist's" funeral, slamming the door.
A billboard memorializes the 71 attacks. A military vehicle roams around the streets reminding the city of curfew, 9 PM to 4 AM. Elliot arrives at Shama's house as her father is packing the car, preparing to move. Arash says he doesn't want trouble as he sends his family inside. Elliot says he went to school with Shama and that she was a good person, insisting she is innocent. Arash asks if he knows why she went to Arizona. Elliot says no. Arash stops his son from eavesdropping and believes her to be a victim of Islamophobia. As Elliot walks away, Arash thanks him for saying nice things about his daughter.
Elliot takes the subway to Coney Island and sits on the beach alone. As he opens his bag of morphine pills, Shama's brother Mohammed appears and asks about it. Mohammed dismisses the idea of needing a babysitter but doesn't know how to get home because he followed Elliot. He sits down, much to Elliot's annoyance. Mohammed asks about why Elliot said Shama was innocent, getting no answer. Elliot ultimately decides to walk the boy home.
Mohammed talks about the mosque that he and Shama went to, telling an anecdote about her tripping putting her shoes back on. They pass a basketball court turned military detention center. Elliot insists that he needs to get back to Coney Island for something important. Mohammed keeps asking questions. At the house, no one answers the door. Mohammed asks more questions, and finally Elliot says he used to like movies. Mohammed has never been to the movies and wants to go. His parents went to go visit his uncle in Connecticut. Elliot asks Mohammed if he's lying but promises to take him to see a movie if something good is playing.
It's Back to the Future day at the theater. Mohammed doesn't know what it is and wants to see The Martian . Elliot says The Martian looks like shit and is surprised that his childhood dream to see Back To The Future Part II on the day Marty goes to the future (Oct. 21, 2015) has presented itself. Elliot puts M&Ms in the popcorn to the initial dismay of the boy, who after tasting it, admits to liking it. In line, Elliot tries to explain the movie to Mohammed, starting a debate among costumed fans about the intricacies of time travel. Elliot dismisses The Martian 's 92% on Rotten Tomatoes as most critics having shitty taste.
During the movie, a person cosplaying as Doc asks Elliot to hold his flux capacitor prop as he cleans his glasses. Afterward, Elliot discovers that Mohammed has disappeared. Out by the concessions, Elliot learns from a worker that the boy left. Elliot notices two people leaving, one of them complaining about her heels. It reminds him of Mohammed's mosque story about Shama tripping while putting on her shoes. A Jewish man named Sy stops his ice cream truck and gives Elliot a ride to the mosque. Elliot notes that the driver is listening to War of the Worlds . He finds it ironic. The driver explains that it actually is about the persevering of humans in the end.
Elliot finds Mohammed alone in the mosque. He questions why he bailed and said he would've brought him here. Mohammed brings up that Elliot said that he had something important to do. Elliot wants to bring the boy home. He is urgent. Their argument ends abruptly when Elliot blurts that he also wishes he were dead. Mohammed sometimes thinks he did something bad to make his sister Shama leave. Elliot consoles him and takes the blame himself. Mohammed tells Elliot to take his shoes off inside. He does and vows not to trip on anything when he puts them back on. Mohammed says that he could be president because he was born in the US, unlike the rest of his family. He says if he were president, he would stay in his own house, bring back his sister, put the real bad guys in jail, make everyone have Pop-Tarts for dinner, and make everyone to be nice to him. Elliot calls him a dictator, defining it as a really bad president. They discuss Elliot's birthplace in NJ. Mohammed reveals he was born in Trenton.
The duo returns to the Biswas house to find that his parents still haven't returned home. Mohammed opens the door with his key. He thanks Elliot for taking him to the movies and asks his name. He apologizes for making him late for his important thing. Mohammed asks to see Elliot again, who promises to take him to The Martian before his family moves. Mohammed tells him to wait while he gets something for Elliot. Elliot begins to cry while waiting. Mohammed gives him a green lollipop because Elliot said he was sick.
Elliot returns to Sandesh's house and tells him to give Sunil a proper funeral. Met with hostility, Elliot reveals that he had hacked him and blackmails him. The morphine he bought from Hard Andy, one of his shady clients, will provide enough money from the funeral by selling it back to Andy. Elliot wants an invitation and vows to be in the back of the funeral, listening for a good eulogy.
Elliot walks through the red tinted hall outside Angela's apartment. He knocks and asks to see if he can talk to her, saying that he's worried about her. She remains silent as he continues, saying he wishes he could snap her out of it. He moves to leave but sits with his back to the door. Elliot reminds her of the wishing game they used to play as kids, as she sits with her back to the door on the other side. They wished for bigger bedrooms, her for more protractors, him for a faster computer, her for better clothes, both for the ability to drive, to drive away on road trips. They closed their eyes and wished. Even though their wishes never came true, the ending wasn't what they cared about, it was the wishing. Angela gets emotional. Elliot didn't get it back then, but what she said to him right before they opened their eyes made it all better. "No matter what happens, we'll be okay," Angela says from behind the door.
Elliot returns home when a white van stops outside and dumps trash, including the Mr. Robot jacket. He takes it back, thinking that deletion isn't always permanent. He replaces his bathroom mirror and installs his new computer. He finds an email from Shama: a way to possibly undo the hack.

EPISODE: S4E01

As the opening recap ends with Angela meeting with Phillip outside his palatial estate, it seamlessly flows into the beginning of the episode. Angela tearfully wants to play a role in retribution against the Whiterose for the E Corp bombings. Phillip tells her to simply learn how to live with it. She declares that she'll do it herself, but when she moves to walk toward the house, something catches her eyes as a door opens and closes. Phillip explains that all he wants is to protect her from the Whiterose, imploring her to beg for forgiveness. Angela tells him to remove his emotions from his panicked state. She returns to the bench, resolute that she will not run. Phillip walks back to the house, removing a hidden microphone from his shirt, as two Dark Army soldiers arrive and shoot Angela in the back of the head.
Inside, Phillip hurls a vase at the floor. He receives a call from the Whiterose, who tells him that Angela made her choice. Phillip blames the Whiterose for recruiting her. The Whiterose accepts his lashing out calmly and ends the call.
On her island, the Whiterose stares out at the ocean and hands the phone to her assistant Wang Shu . Wang informs her that Elliot's shipment hack will deliver the project by the end of the year, in two months time. Wang says that Elliot cannot be trusted. The Whiterose says that once the project is delivered, Elliot can be terminated. Wang says that he must be kept on a short leash and trained to not bite his master. The Whiterose allows her to send him a reminder of the consequences.
It's December 21, Christmastime in NYC. At a holiday party at the office of Lomax & Looney Law , Freddy Lomax is being a sexist jerk to his assistant, who gives him a package. The letter disturbs him enough to send him to his office. On his TV, he plays the CD he just received of his sexual video chat with an underage girl. The phone rings from inside the package. Freddy answers Mr. Robot 's call. He directs him to open his email. Freddy tries to barter for silence, but Mr. Robot does not care about money. Freddy is forced to copy his email inbox onto a USB drive before leaving his electronics behind and heading to Grand Central Station. Mr. Robot watches from outside.
Freddy gets into a cab. The news on TV covers the economic boom from the 5/9 reversal . The praise falls on E Corp, E Coin, and CTO Tyrell Wellick .
Inside Grand Central Station, Freddy is guided by the all-seeing eye of Mr. Robot to buy a ticket from the furthest kiosk as Dark Army operatives arrive on scene. The coke-addled lawyer is anxious, but Mr. Robot coaches him on how to lose the tail: by throwing a wad of money into a busker's case so the Dark Army will frantically search it for a moment. Freddy is directed to a train car where Elliot waits with his laptop.
Freddy pulls a gun on Elliot, but Elliot has the video ready to be sent to the FBI and Freddy's family. Elliot looks through Freddy's emails and attachments. He tracks the money Freddy funnels for Zhi Zhang (the Whiterose) to Cyprus National Bank . Elliot pushes him for more information, a contact, though he claims to be a low-level paper pusher. Freddy gives the name John Garcin . He says that the address is at his office. Elliot notices that the Dark Army soldiers are coming toward the train and realizes that Freddy's ID tag is Bluetooth enabled. Elliot has them split up to rendezvous outside while leaving the tag in the car. Over the phone, Freddy is fearful of the Dark Army. Hearing Elliot's silence indicating that he can't protect him, Freddy kills himself with his gun on the street corner. Elliot runs to join the crowd around the body.
December 22, the next day, Tyrell walks into E Corp as his assistant Elizabeth informs him of his busy day of meetings and appearances. In his office, he asks to postpone anything until tomorrow. He can't. He asks for a minute. Elizabeth thanks him for his heroism. Alone, Tyrell stares ahead blankly.
At her mom's house, Dominique looks like a wreck struggling to stay awake in the middle of the day. She is suspicious of a car parked in the driveway. Peeking out of her door, she sees a strange man ascending the stairs. She gets her gun and confronts him. Her mom, Trudy , finds them and explains that he's renovating the bathroom, as she told her last week she planned to have done. Dominique insists that she vet anyone her mom hires. Trudy laughs it off and goes to go the mall walking with Janice , who she met at church and wants to set up with Dominique. Trudy tells her that Janice is coming over for dinner.
In the now abandoned Allsafe office, Mr. Robot searches through John Garcin's boring social media while Elliot adds his name to a conspiracy web. Elliot wants to go to his address, believing him to be a liaison to Cyprus National Bank, while Mr. Robot wants to do more research to break him as they always do. Elliot won't wait another two weeks, as the Whiterose will kill them once her project is delivered. Elliot ignores a call from Darlene . Mr. Robot takes note of Elliot's cold demeanor. He tells Elliot to put aside his own anger. Elliot explains that if they rob the bank, they will stop the Whiterose. Mr. Robot claims what they once started to save the world is now clouded about his feelings for Angela. Elliot points it out that society has forgotten about 5/9 and the bombings in place of Christmas commercialism and that if they don't do something, the Whiterose will get away with it. Elliot is done with his feelings; his only focus is the Whiterose. Mr. Robot reads a text from Darlene, telling Elliot about Angela.
At his apartment, Elliot lets in Darlene, who is frantic. She asks about Flipper . Elliot gave him to his landlord for the week. Darlene wonders what her brother is busy with. She goes on to say that she thinks she saw Angela. Elliot is dismissive. Mr. Robot tells her that Angela is gone and asks if Darlene is on drugs. Darlene dodges the question. She recounts seeing Angela at a shelter but losing her in the crowd. Her body was never found, after all. Darlene insists that she was wearing her same crazy outfit from before she was taken. Elliot blames the cocaine. Darlene fights with him for shutting down. Elliot gets in her face, declaring that Angela is dead and it's not their fault. Darlene leaves. Mr. Robot asks why on he didn't just show Darlene the photo the Whiterose sent of Angela's body. We see a quick flash of the image. Elliot didn't want to break her heart. Now he wants to get back to work.
Mr. Robot begins narrating to the audience as he watches Elliot gather documents. He explains that Elliot hasn't been talking much since Angela's death. Distracting himself from the pain, like everyone does during the holidays. Mr. Robot rants about Christmas fakeness while they travel. He admits to bringing in the audience not because he likes them, but because Elliot does.
They arrive at an apartment building owned by E Corp. Mr. Robot wants to be cautious, but Elliot heads in. Inside, the security guard pours a bowl of cereal while a nearby man talks loudly on FaceTime in Samoan. Elliot tells the security guard that he has a delivery for John Garcin. The guard directs them upstairs. There, they find the apartment door ajar. They enter, close the door, and search all over the place, though Mr. Robot reminds Elliot the plan was to just take over the Wi-Fi. No one is there, and the apartment appears staged: everything is covered in dust and there's no sign anyone ever lived there. They realize the door is now locked and the phone signal is jammed. Elliot finds a book on the shelf, No Exit by Jean-Paul Sartre. He realizes that "John Garcin" is a name taken from the book and that they were set up by Freddy. It's a honeypot.
The guard plays "Don't Worry Be Happy" by Bobby McFerrin on an old iPod while two men drag Elliot away.

Janice seems embarrassed. Trudy calls it a night and asks Dominique to help Janice take the leftovers home. Janice says that Dominique has put it off for weeks and it looks suspicious. She says unless Dominique cleans up Santiago's mess, Janice will kill her mother. Dominique threatens Janice with death if she touches her mom. Janice laughs it off, saying killing her won't stop the others. Dominique notices the vans down the street.

She then collapses on the bed and cries.

The events of the past year flash before his eyes before they close. The credits briefly begin before the episode resumes. Someone sprays Narcan into Elliot's nose, rousing him. It's the three men. Phillip Price walks in. "Welcome back, Mr. Alderson."

A test pattern on a TV screen is shown. Phillip narrates that when the Berlin Wall fell in 1989, and the Soviet Union soon after, the world was up for grabs. People put all their information online. The Whiterose began construction of her billion dollar machine underneath Washington Township. Phillip eventually realized that they were all working for her.

At the funeral home, Elliot receives a call from Phillip. He has played his hand and now they wait. Elliot thanks him, but Phillip isn't doing it for him. Darlene enters with the urn. He needs everything Darlene has on her, as Susan worked with the Dark Army . Darlene is shocked to hear that Elliot is going after the Whiterose, saying that it's suicide. She discerns that Elliot is trying to protect her, even at the inevitable cost of his own life. Darlene wants to join him. She links their phones to share their locations.

In 1982, IBM executives are in a meeting with a Chinese executive, Zhi Zhang , and his translator, Chen . The Americans want to finalize a deal to open a facility in Asia. The Chinese men are largely ignoring them, sharing romantic notions in their own language. The deal is reached, and the executive jokes (in Mandarin) how he'll enjoy stealing IBM's intellectual property. Later, Zhang and Chen are having a romantic moment in a hotel room. They are looking forward to Zhang becoming the ambassador to the US so they can move to a country where they can be themselves. Chen's watch beeps, annoying Zhang. Their next meeting is in 15 minutes, so Chen leaves to take a shower. When he returns, Zhang tells him to go alone. They kiss.
When Chen returns later that night, Zhang tells him not to turn on the light. Zhang appears in a wig and dress: "It was my mother's." Zhang admires its simplicity and elegance. Chen calls Zhang beautiful and they kiss. In the present, Minister Zhang hangs up the dress and tells Wang Shu that he wants it ready to wear on the day the project ships. Wang warns him of celebrating too early. Freddy Lomax 's suicide coincided with a hacker taking over Grand Central, not an easy feat. At the same time, Phillip wants to resign. It's not a coincidence, it's Elliot's next move. Zhang says to refuse Phillip's demands and surveil Elliot. Wang tells Zhang to have patience. The word bothers Zhang.
Sometime later in the past, Chinese people are having an extravagant party. Zhang asks the bride-to-be about the groom and finds him in the dressing room. The groom-to-be, Chen, is distressed, as his father is forcing him to marry the woman to keep up appearances. Chen wants to leave China. Zhang tries to convince him to put on a good show for his father, and later they can be together. They discuss that Zhang was not made US ambassador but Minister of State Security, so he will be able amass power in Beijing. He tells Chen to be patient, but Chen thinks to be patient is to surrender. Zhang assures him that since Zhang trusted him with his secret, they will make a better world. They kiss, but the groom needs a moment. He grabs a knife. He declares the world will never be good enough and cuts his own throat, blood spraying on the white roses, a joke Zhang sent to him as funeral flowers. Zhang screams in terror over the body.
In the present, Zhang says to arrange a Deus Group meeting tomorrow to give Phillip his resignation. Wang says that it cannot be done on Christmas. Zhang wants to destabilize Phillip's timeline and force him into a mistake. They will call Tyrell Wellick and make him CEO, on the orders of the Whiterose. Zhang gazes longingly at the dress.
Elliot and Mr. Robot are walking on the sidewalk. Mr. Robot narrates that playing Russian roulette, hearing the click, the sound of cheating death, changes you. He wonders what Vera's up to. Elliot won't listen to anything, putting up his Forbidden Error on the walls. They run into Krista and her friend Jason . Elliot tries to talk with her, to thank her and say that he's doing better, but Krista insists that she will take legal action if he makes contact with her. As Elliot walks away, a man on a cell phone follows.

Darlene notes that Elliot chose Allsafe for emotional reasons, while he dismisses it as technical. He explains that Olivia's ex-husband has their kid tonight, and she has a date at a bar. Darlene doesn't want to be sidelined and wants to do the breaking and entering thing. Elliot lets Mr. Robot try to talk some sense into her. She lights a cigarette at the thought of danger. Elliot grabs her hard. She is alarmed, asking if it's really him. She concludes that their relationship will never change and he won't get better. He says he never should've opened the door when she came back to town.

Elliot searches the bathroom and finds a bottle of Oxycontin. In the bedroom, he unlocks a drawer and hacks her work laptop. Mr. Robot looks through the lame social media of her date, a man named Evan Floyd . Elliot finds that her laptop has high security. Mr. Robot wonders if she left her USB key around the place. Elliot notes that she's a single mom who's worked hard to get where she is, so she isn't that careless. Elliot looks at the picture of Evan Floyd.

Olivia agrees, for Christmas. The USB key is clipped to her bag.

Mr. Robot kept the happy memories, hiding the truth to protect himself as much as Elliot, afraid of how it might hurt him. Mr. Robot apologizes for keeping Elliot in the dark. And if he must be gone for good, Mr. Robot wants him to know that he is not, nor ever was, Elliot's father. Elliot knows, that he created him to be the father he needed, not the one he had. Mr. Robot starts to say that if he could go back in time and stop all of this from happening. . . . But Elliot counters that he wouldn't be who he is today, and he wouldn't have Mr. Robot. As Mr. Robot puts his hands on Elliot's shoulders, Elliot says that he can't do the hack. He can't do anything. Elliot begins weeping.

EPISODE: S4E09
======================================================================

A door below an exit sign opens and Mr. Robot comes through. He walks down a long hallway and through an identical door. He enters a meeting room where a young version of Elliot's mother, Magda Alderson , and a younger version of Elliot sit at the round table. Magda asks him, "How is he?" Mr. Robot says that it isn't going to happen today so there's no point in waiting; They need to help him through this. Magda wants to bring him here. Young Elliot asks him if they should tell him everything. Mr. Robot declines again. Magda says Mr. Robot has let this go on for too long. Mr. Robot says they just have to finish Elliot's hack, and then they can get through. Magda asks how. Mr. Robot replies, "Show him what he did." Magda says they can't go on like this if it doesn't work and that they may lose the poor boy forever. Mr. Robot says he woke up when Darlene talked to him two months ago. She is the key.
Darlene is in a hotel room, prepping for the hack on a laptop. Mr. Robot enters, narrating that he is here while Elliot is dealing with his mental trauma. Mr. Robot notes that the Deus Group should be arriving soon. Darlene asks where's he's been, but Mr. Robot simply says that he was held up. Darlene asserts she had a bad day too. As they bicker, Darlene realizes that's she's with Mr. Robot and asks what happened. Mr. Robot says that Elliot will tell her when he's ready. There is a knock at the door. Phillip enters. Mr. Robot says this is risky, as the Deus Group meeting is right across the street. Phillip says that he needs a favor and hands over a thumb drive. He asks Mr. Robot to promise to destroy the Whiterose 's machine, as Angela wanted. Mr. Robot agrees. He tells Phillip to keep everyone at the meeting while they hack their phones. Phillip leaves. Darlene is surprised that Phillip knows Angela. Later, Phillip is narrating the plan to steal the numbers and the bank accounts. Phillip approaches the Deus Group meeting. Inside, in an open space museum floor, Phillip finds Zhang sitting at a table for two.
Darlene sits at her laptop, wondering aloud why Angela never told her that Phillip was her father. Mr. Robot says that maybe she didn't know. Darlene states that she misses Angela. Mr. Robot is watching the Deus Group guards from the window. He finds it suspicious that no one has entered or left except Phillip. Darlene wonders if their plan has been discovered. Phillip is patted down by the masked Dark Army soldiers. Zhang wants to have a drink. Phillip wants to skip the foreplay.
Mr. Robot says they have been found out. If the Deus Group doesn't show up, it's over. He concludes that Elliot would look for abnormalities. He goes on the laptop and recalls that Elliot saved an image on Tyrell 's phone. Zhang decries that Phillip couldn't wait until the new year and that he would have been allowed to live in retirement. Darlene takes the laptop and starts looking at Tyrell's calendar. Zhang asks what Phillip and Elliot were working on and if Phillip reveals it, he will be allowed to go home and die in his sleep. Otherwise, they have their methods. Darlene finds the image, a different location for the Deus Group meeting. Mr. Robot muses that if Phillip is the only one who got the other address, the guards aren't there to just kill him, they're there to protect someone else. Zhang gloats that the meeting is taking place as they speak and Tyrell is impressing everyone. Phillip says that he expects a mutiny because Tyrell isn't there. Darlene wants to go to the new location. Mr. Robot wants to stay and keep an eye on the Whiterose. Darlene doesn't want to know if the plan goes wrong, and they only have one device to catch the numbers. Mr. Robot sends her off.
Wang Shu confirms that Tyrell is not at the meeting. Zhang is angry, asking where Tyrell is. Phillip doesn't know, continuing to drink. Wang wants to go to the meeting, as Phillip is nothing but a fool. Zhang refuses. Wang insists that letting Elliot live has led them to this delay. She tells Zhang that Elliot has beat him and they must warn the Deus Group. When Zhang refuses again, Wang quits and walks out.
Darlene is at the new location, a restaurant called Cipriani. Inside, the room is filled with Deus Group members. The kitchen staff is busy. A worker goes outside for a cigarette, but a guard tells her to go back inside, that the area is secured. Darlene watches from the barricades at the corner. She is distraught at the level of security, but notices a nearby building being used to film "Shift + Control," a TV show inspired by fsociety .
Mr. Robot grabs his phone. He calls Phillip's phone and Zhang picks up. They exchange a few words, then Zhang offers to reveal something about Angela if he stops his plot. Zhang says Angela is not dead. Mr. Robot reminds him he saw the picture of her corpse. Zhang insists that she is alive and not to believe everything he sees. Zhang can take Elliot to see her, hear her voice, hold her hand. Suddenly, it is Elliot holding the phone. Zhang offers to show Elliot a world without his pain or regrets. Elliot sheds a tear, saying he saw what Angela became because of the Whiterose's using her. Zhang says to ask her yourself. Elliot receives a message from Darlene to turn on the TV.
The news shows a new fsociety video. Darlene has donned the mask and reveals to the camera that the Deus Group runs the world. She has doxxed them, linking their private files, and inviting people to the meeting location. Zhang is furious. Elliot gets a call from Darlene. The fsociety video will smoke them out, Darlene says. Elliot tells her that he had spoken to the Whiterose. Darlene asks if he's okay and is glad that he's back. Elliot notices a cell tower nearby and enacts a plan to get the numbers. Zhang is on the phone, calming down the Deus Group members, telling them not to go outside. They hang up. Zhang yells at Phillip. Elliot is hacking while Darlene hacks the restaurant's garage barricade. At the meeting, one member starts to leave, starting a rush for the exit. Their cars are trapped in the garage because of a jammer Darlene has left behind. The Deus Group members spill into the back alley. Darlene watches from the barricade as a crowd swarms. Darlene hacks on her phone. She is capturing people's numbers while Elliot phishes for access to the cell tower. He is successful. The garage barricade is opened manually. Zhang is pacing, wondering if the front entrance is secure and demanding the car be brought. Phillip marvels at what havoc a pipsqueak in a hoodie has wrought. Elliot is hacking. Mr. Robot asks for an update. They have a bunch of people's numbers, but don't know if the Whiterose is among them. Darlene has captured 99 of 100 Deus Group accounts. She checks with Elliot. Phillip rubs it in Zhang's face that Elliot is the only one who could truly hurt him.
Zhang and Phillip exit the museum. Phillip stops on the stairs to take in the cold, peaceful night. Zhang asks if Phillip must be forced into the car. Phillip admits that he almost believed that Angela was still alive. But he knows Zhang is a con man. Darlene finds the final account. She tells Elliot to start the bank transfer. Cars begin picking up the Deus Group members. One of the men receives a text from the bank with a 2FA code. Elliot intercepts it. Phillip tells Zhang that Angela lives on in the people who love her and have set off to destroy Zhang. The money transfer is complete. Elliot marvels with Mr. Robot. Zhang receives the message on his phone as Phillip concludes that they are broke. Zhang yells as the accounts are overdrawn. Phillip tells Zhang that his project, his dream of another world, is all but dead. Zhang grabs a gun from a Dark Army soldier and shoots Phillip multiple times. Elliot and Mr. Robot arrive on the sidewalk across the street to see Phillip fall dead. Mr. Robot narrates that Rome has fallen: no more top 1% playing gods. As one Deus Group member is driven away, his picture is being taken by the crowd. He sees Darlene in the crowd. Elliot puts on his hoodie and walks away as Zhang looks in his direction before being driven away.
In her residence, the Whiterose applies lipstick as the police bang on the front door. They demand that Zhang open up, count down, and bust down the doors, and they and the guards start exchanging gunfire.

A news anchor (Gretchen Carlson) explains that of the data dump from fsociety doxxing the Deus Group , a few documents have been substantiated but intelligence agencies caution about believing them as a whole. She tells Darlene that going to Budapest was Francis' dream. Darlene offers that they can go somewhere else. She says she can't handle things alone because she will have a panic attack. If she leaves the airport, she will just go back to the grind. Dominique hugs Darlene. She asks for a postcard and writes down the number of a friend at US Cyber Command. Darlene is gripping the bathroom counter tight, hyperventilating. The last call for boarding goes over the PA. The stranger asks if she needs help, noticing it's her flight being called. She offers to call someone for help. Darlene, her breathing slowing, says that she can take care of herself. On the plane with Otto Irving's book in her hand, Dominique sleeps.
